Business Tax Reporting and Calculation Methods 108

Various Industry Tax Rules Committees Write to Request Explanation

The Tax Rules Research Committee of various industry trade associations in the city sent a letter to the Business Tax Collection Office of the Municipal Finance Bureau yesterday requesting an explanation of the business tax reporting procedures and calculation methods. The letter stated, "Regarding business tax in this city, implementation is imminent, but detailed handling is always welcome. We urgently need to request explanations on the following points, which are enumerated below: (1) Article 2 of the Implementing Rules of the Business Tax Regulations in this city states that those who meet the requirements for collecting business tax should apply for a business tax investigation certificate. According to the meaning of the provisions, those who do not meet the tax requirements can naturally not apply for a business tax investigation certificate. The clear statement in your office's reply to the City Chamber of Commerce approving the postponement of the grain store industry's application for an investigation certificate further leaves no doubt. However, in addition to the grain store industry, there are other tax-exempt businesses in the city, such as the tap water industry, the water sales industry, the garment industry, the lace embroidery industry, and the restaurant industry that is located near schools and specializes in selling student meals. Those that have been revised and deleted include the car rental industry, the contracted meal industry, and various industries that have already paid property tax, deed tax, slaughter tax, and other taxes that are the same as business tax. None of these meet the tax requirements and naturally do not need to apply for a business tax investigation certificate. This is the first point for your instructions. (2) Article 2 of the Business Tax Law and Article 20 of the Business Tax Regulations of this city both state that the brokerage industry will temporarily be taxed at the old tax rate. However, the brokerage industry in this city is located in the Chinese area and has all received brokerage licenses. Changing to business tax is certainly difficult. Those established in the concession area may not all have brokerage licenses, so the tax rate will be impossible to calculate. If the standard for taxation is based on their business turnover, then the very meager commissions they receive will not be enough to pay the taxes. It is only fair and in line with the principle of business tax emphasizing revenue to base the taxation on the commission amount. Moreover, according to the business tax rate in this city, the auction industry has already set a precedent for taxing based on the commission amount, which seems to be feasible. This is the second point for your instructions. (3) Items 6 and 8 of the business registration form in this city have estimated annual business income. The so-called estimate is the amount of business expected at the beginning of the year. The business of stores has its ups and downs, and it is difficult to make an accurate estimate. However, ordinary stores are not so different unless they encounter special changes, while the construction industry is very different. Some have last year's business turnover of millions of yuan, while this year there is no business income at all. Some have no business income last year, while this year's business turnover is millions of yuan. The degree of difference is tenfold or a hundredfold. If the estimate is too high, it will frequently increase the extra burden. If the estimate is too low, it may affect the government's tax revenue, which is not a good strategy for both parties. Moreover, the construction of contracted buildings often takes several years to complete. It is also difficult to calculate the tax on the result of a business tax once a year. Recently, the industry has repeatedly reported the difficult situation in person and intends to treat the contracting of a building as setting up a branch store, applying for a business tax investigation certificate and hanging it at the location of the building, and paying business tax according to the contract amount. In this way, both the taxpayer and the tax collector will be fair, and the difficulty of calculating taxes will be easily solved. The Association observes that the situation is real. In order to take into account both facts and laws, there is no other way to seek it. This is the third point for your instructions. (4) Article 9 of the Business Tax Regulations of this city states that manufacturers who sell their manufactured products directly at their manufacturing sites will still be taxed at the tax rate prescribed for the manufacturing industry. Does the so-called manufacturing site only refer to the factory site, or does it refer to the city area? If it is limited to the factory site, the burden on manufacturers seems to be too heavy, which is contrary to the national government's purpose of supporting enterprises. This is the fourth point for your instructions. Regarding the above points, we respectfully request that your office reply to each one for guidance."

Aviator Le Yuge Returns from France 109

Mr. Le Yuge, a native of Peiping, is 24 years old this year. In the thirteenth year of the Republic (1924), he entered a middle school in Paris. After graduating, he transferred to the Morane-Saulnier flight school in France. Mr. Le is talented and has a strong physique. He has always had a research interest in flying airplanes. Since entering this school, he has been instructed by Michael Tlai (the world's first in aviation). His studies have progressed rapidly, and he soars freely in the sky. No one can surpass him. Therefore, he graduated this summer, and all the large and small exams were ranked at the top. In the country, he is a rare talent. It is heard that Mr. Le will return to Peiping from Shanghai soon to visit his relatives. In the future, he will use his knowledge and skills, and he will surely make immeasurable contributions to the aviation industry of the society and the country.

Searching for Lost Boy 110

Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, a boy named Yuan Yuan, also known as Liu Sheng, aged four, went missing from No. 140 Huaxing Lane, Yongxing Road, Zhabei. He has a white and round face, and was wearing a short wool jacket, willow-colored white trousers, red cloth shoes, and old western socks. After the family discovered his disappearance, they searched everywhere, but there was no trace of him. His parents are heartbroken. Anyone who knows his whereabouts is requested to notify the above address, and a reward will be given.

Japanese Overseas Aggression and Overseas Chinese Publishing 111

The book "Japanese Overseas Aggression and Overseas Chinese" is written by Mr. Liu Shimu. Mr. Liu has been researching Southeast Asia for twenty years and considers it his life's work. He has traveled to Southeast Asia, England, the Netherlands, and France three times to conduct field investigations. Therefore, the content of this book focuses entirely on the collection and writing of facts. The book "Japanese Overseas Aggression and Overseas Chinese" is tightly focused in every word and deeply painful in every stroke. It is an unprecedented masterpiece introducing the situation in Southeast Asia. It does not engage in empty lofty arguments. Everything about the Japanese policy, process, and steps of advancing into Southeast Asia, as well as their sharp eyes and powerful methods, such as the competition in shipping and fishing, the seizure of financial markets, the secret surveillance of the status of Chinese businessmen, the operation of small peddlers, and the intimidation of rulers and alliances with natives, is fully available. Even the scandalous traces, anecdotes, secrets, and unpublished stories are widely collected and integrated into a grand spectacle. If one can hold this volume in hand, one can not only use it to examine the courage of the Japanese in advancing into Southeast Asia, but also to observe the safety of the status of Overseas Chinese, and also to understand the truth of various businesses in Southeast Asia. It is truly an outstanding work for studying the Southeast Asian issue. The price per volume is one yuan, and it is sold at the Shanghai and provincial Commercial Press.

Letter to the Editor 126

Dear Sir, I have read in the news column of your newspaper on the 19th that Shen Aizhen, a piano teacher at Moore Memorial Church, committed suicide. After investigation, there is no such person as Shen Aizhen among the piano teachers in our church, and her name is not even found in the student register. I believe it is a mistake in your newspaper's reporting. I am afraid of misunderstandings from the outside world, so I specially request a correction. Sincerely, Moore Memorial Church.

| 3-1 Victory in Final Against Wang Sun

The men's doubles tennis final saw Yu Tianguang and Liu Keng defeat Wang Minqin and Sun Chengbi with a score of 3-1. The performance of both sides lacked brilliance, with many errors, making it a rather ordinary match. The referee was Tang Zhongguang.

Match Details

First set: The competition was fierce, with the scores very close. At 4-4, Yu and Liu gained another game to lead 5-4. However, they then lost three consecutive games, ultimately losing the set 5-7. In this set, Liu Keng made many errors, hitting the net frequently, and Yu Tianguang was also not performing strongly. The loss was entirely due to self-inflicted errors. Wang and Sun, particularly Sun Chengbi, played powerfully, with frequent smashes, leading to Yu and Liu's initial defeat.

Second set: Yu and Liu took the lead at 5-4, but Wang and Sun won back two games, making it 5-6. Yu and Liu also won two games, making it 7-6. At this crucial juncture, the outcome was still uncertain. After 7-7, Yu and Liu fought bravely to win 9-7. In this set, Yu Tianguang gradually improved, hitting with force, and Sun Chengbi's smashes also frequently hit the net.

Last two sets: To maintain their lead, Yu and Liu played with extraordinary caution. The opponents also wanted to regain the victory. As a result, in the doubles match, Yu and Wang were seen exchanging long baseline shots, while Liu and Sun watched from the sidelines, or Yu and Sun traded long shots, with neither daring to approach the net. This was a rare sight. In the final two sets, Yu and Liu gradually rallied, while Wang Minshi was poor at running and dealing with backhand shots, making it difficult to cope. Sun Chengbi was less steady than in the first two sets. Consequently, Yu and Liu won with scores of 6-2 and 6-4.

Championship Winning Situation

| Turning Point of the Second Set |

In the first set, Yang took a 4-2 lead, but Xiang won back two games to tie the score at 4-4. Yang then won two more games to win the set. Yang's victory came with ease, with excellent forehand and backhand shots, making her likely to win. In the second set, Yang again took a 4-1 lead, with Xiang only winning the second game. Although Xiang fought to 3-4, Yang surged ahead again, needing just one more game to win the championship. However, the opposite happened. Yang's performance declined sharply from then on. Since she was not good at running, she gave up on many balls. Xiang's momentum became fierce, and many balls hit Yang's racket but could not be returned. Xiang won four consecutive games, completely reversing the situation and rising to prominence. In the deciding third set, Xiang won three consecutive games, then took a 4-1 lead, reversing the downward trend of the first set. Yang had too many weak shots and errors. Although she fought hard to save the situation, Xiang ultimately won the third set 6-4 and the championship 2-1. Xiang's victory was entirely due to brute force, while Yang lost due to carelessness. Both players still need to further develop their skills, as their variations were not diverse.

Jinan Wins Soccer Championship 132

Superior Throughout, Fighting Spirit High

| Jinan Wins 5-1 |

Jinan Football has dominated Shanghai for years. The team viewed this Shanghai Municipal Football Championship as being in their grasp. Their only formidable rival was the Youyou team. Since the start of the competition, Jinan and Youyou had been like two dragons entering the sea, thrashing and struggling forward amidst towering waves. By yesterday, the time was ripe for them to seize the pearl. The twenty-two heroes from both sides lined up at the China baseball field. Under the refereeing of He Chunhui, they battled for ninety minutes. Jinan displayed overwhelming momentum and achieved their wish, winning the championship with a score of five to one. Youyou fought throughout, with high morale. Regardless of victory or defeat, they were commendable.

(1) The Journey of the Heroes to Seize the Championship

(2) Each Had Its Merits

However, their actions were also rough, which was inevitable. Jiang Shanjing's defense of the last line was a great achievement. He was steady and tough, and had few lapses, showing even more progress than before. The three players in the center defense line were excellent, and there was nothing to add. The five forwards formed a line, and their advance and retreat were well-ordered. Luo Haiguang and Qiu Dongyan were the pillars of this formation, making many contributions. Free Talk

Random Notes by Bu Chu Ting Cao Zhai Fu

Living Husband (Part 1) 143

Among insects, praying mantises, spiders, scorpions, and others eat their husbands alive, with the praying mantis being the most brutal. French entomologist Jean-Henri Fabre (born 1823, died 1915) observed the love life of the praying mantis (Mantis) as follows:

"Observe their mating. To avoid disturbances from the crowd, we let them live in pairs. Each married couple has a small home, with no idlers disturbing their honeymoon. Plenty of food is also prepared, so they can eat whatever they want, without any hunger.

"It's nearly the end of August. The male praying mantis, a slender lover, believes the time is ripe and aims at his partner. He bends his neck, thrusts out his chest, and his small, pointed face expresses ardent emotion. He stares at his intended without moving, as if she is showing indifference. The male receives this tacit hint (I truly do not know the mystery within) and approaches her, suddenly spreads his wings, and his whole body trembles. This is probably a proposal. Though his body is small, he rushes onto his plump wife's back and holds on firmly. They prepare for a long time before finally mating, and the mating process can sometimes last five or six hours.

"This motionless couple is worth noting. They separate for a moment and then re-engage, even more intimately than before. The lady loves her poor husband not only because he can fertilize her ovaries but also because his flesh suits her taste. Sooner or later, she will catch her husband, bite off his head as usual, and eat it carefully. Everything but the wings will be eaten clean by her."

The Lindbergh Couple's Flight to China 144

– Mo Yi

The American aviator Lindbergh and his wife set off from the United States on July 28 to travel to the Far East. They will be in Japan for nearly a month. According to reports, they will first fly to China on the 19th, directly to Nanjing. At that time, the warm welcome from all sectors of the capital will give this world-famous aviator a new impression. Recently, Western newspapers carried anecdotes about the Lindbergh couple and rumors that they would not come to Shanghai. Here is a translated excerpt:

Not Coming to Shanghai: Last Wednesday, Lindbergh contacted the Shanghai Wan Geng Petroleum Company to request that they prepare twenty gallons of gasoline each in Tianjin and Nanjing between the 14th and 19th for his use. He did not mention whether he would come to Shanghai. The US Consul General in Shanghai, Mr. Cunningham, found this strange and telegraphed Lindbergh, but has received no reply. The reason is unknown. According to several aviators in Shanghai who are familiar with Lindbergh, "We may have the opportunity to see the Lindbergh couple, but to avoid the warm welcome and unnecessary socializing in Shanghai, they may come to Shanghai quietly, thus creating this mystery."

Indifferent to Fame and Fortune: Those in Shanghai who know Lindbergh well say that he has changed his nature somewhat since becoming famous. He sees others making meaningless flattery towards him, and treats even close friends with disdain. Even presidents and emperors are the same. At that time, countless beauties were attracted to him, and millions of gold were readily available, but he discarded them like worn-out shoes and was not moved in the slightest. As a result, his fame grew, and more people respected him, which only increased his aversion. He believes that the most unfortunate thing was that the President of the United States and the Prince of Wales bestowed honors and positions upon him, forcing him to fly back to Central America to escape. When he returned, he often disguised himself when going out; otherwise, he would face the dilemma of being unable to move freely in New York City. He once wore a tattered hat pulled down to his eyebrows and dark glasses on his nose, accompanying his wife to the theater to watch a play. However, he was recognized, and the audience shifted their attention from the play to the couple. Lindbergh was embarrassed and fled without waiting for the curtain to close.

Sweet Times: After Lindbergh crossed the Atlantic, he received a warm welcome from people in the United States and France. Among them was a woman named Annie Morrow, who was particularly attracted to him and once proclaimed herself as the future Mrs. Lindbergh. Lindbergh initially had no fame. Once he became famous, countless women worshipped him as an idol. In 1929, he flew to Mexico and met Miss Annie Morrow, daughter of the former US Ambassador to Mexico, Mr. Morrow. They fell in love and married on May 27 at the Morrow family's villa in Englewood, New Jersey. To avoid newspaper reporters, the wedding was extremely secret, and no one knew about it. Miss Morrow had her wish fulfilled, and the lovers became a family. The joy of their marital chamber must be even greater than the joy of painting eyebrows.

The Birth of Little Lindbergh: Lindbergh's son was born last year. Newspaper offices competed with each other, using great effort to obtain photos of Little Lindbergh and publish them in the newspapers. Lindbergh's feelings towards newspaper reporters have always been incompatible, so he is both praised and criticized. Those who criticize him often exaggerate, straying far from the facts. However, Lindbergh does not bother to correct them, because facts are facts, and any malicious criticism is not worth the attention of those who know.

A Word of Wisdom 145

A pair of old leather shoes can be recycled. A middle-aged woman cannot inspire ardent love in a young man.

Those who like to comment on people's beauty are probably not beautiful themselves. Those who like to discuss people's shortcomings are probably not outstanding themselves.

In the past, secrecy was emphasized in love between the sexes. Now, openness is emphasized. Secrecy and openness have resulted in many heartbroken young men and women in modern times.

Frivolous youths see school as a prison. Romantic women see the family as a temporary lodging.

Seeking physical love with prostitutes is like exercising after a full meal; the harm is extreme.

Cats and dogs without intelligence cannot be loved by humans. How can women without beauty attract men?

Men are not necessarily attracted to women, but a woman's entire being contains colors that attract men. (Xu Xiaoting)

Random Notes from the North Station 146

— Ai Cheng

On the Beijing-Shanghai line, the coming and going of important people is very frequent. Every Saturday, the 9:30 AM express train will have empty flower cars and sleeping cars attached, waiting for use in Beijing. The flower cars used by various important people are mostly designated. Mr. Song Ziwen uses M2, and Chairman Chiang uses PC105. No one is allowed to borrow them on weekdays. Chairman Chiang's flower car is divided into four parts: a reception room, a bedroom, a bathroom, and a servant's bedroom. It is equipped with many sofas, exquisite murals on the walls, deeply hidden embroidered curtains, and bright lights. It is no different from a first-class hotel. Because the chairman does not come to Shanghai often, the car remains at the station almost all year round, which is a great pity.

The railway staff's method of donating salaries for disaster relief has been recorded in this publication. Now, because this method conflicts with the one promulgated by the central government, it has been modified. However, employees with a monthly salary of less than one hundred yuan should still make their own donations separately, solicited by the section chiefs. In the past day or two, the number has been quite considerable. Even track workers and stokers who earn only ten or so yuan a month are enthusiastically contributing, with a minimum of one yuan and a maximum of ten or twenty yuan. It can be said that they are acting bravely and righteously.

Mr. Zhang Ransheng, the former chief of the railway, served for more than thirty years. Unfortunately, he was dismissed during Director Cai's tenure. Now, Director Guo has reported to the Ministry of Railways and approved his return, appointing him as the chief of both railways. On the day he took office, the workers pooled their money to buy over a thousand firecrackers. At 7:00 AM, they waited for Mr. Zhang to arrive at the bureau and set off the firecrackers everywhere, the sound reverberating through the sky and the cheers echoing. Mr. Zhang was deeply touched by this.

In recent days, the Yangtze River has risen again. The Nanjing riverside station has been submerged by the raging waves, and the tracks are no longer visible. The platform is also in imminent danger. The stationmaster, finding transportation difficult, intends to cancel the Jinpu Railway joint transportation. The head of the transportation department, Yuan Shaochang, believes that the joint transportation is related to the Shanghai market and has not yet approved it.

A Study of American Wheat Varieties 147

— Chen Yangnian

The severity of the flood in our country this time is rare in centuries. The issue of wheat varieties in the flood has been mentioned in previous reports. According to the opinion of Dr. Love of the United States, American wheat is not suitable for Chinese soil and climate. Planting American wheat by mistake would be unimaginable. We should quickly collect existing wheat varieties. In practice, we have found this to be quite untrue. Ten years ago, when I was in Shanghai, I received a peck of American white wheat from my old friend Mao Ziheng. I took it back to Jiangzhou, Zhenjiang, and the results of the trial planting for more than ten years have shown that the grains are round, the stems are thick, and the variety does not change at all. In the spring and summer, when walking leisurely in the fields, seeing the American wheat with thick stems, strong ears, and a shiny green color, it is very different from the thin and short Chinese wheat. Therefore, it is easy to tell that it is a good variety. The above situation of trial planting American wheat is based on personal experience and differs greatly from what Dr. Love of the United States said. I don't know what Dr. Love's basis for saying that is. In my opinion, American wheat is suitable for Chinese soil and there is no need to discuss it further. However, the most important thing to note is the planting time of American wheat, which must be ten days before the frost season, the earlier the better. Harvesting can only be done during the awn season of the following year. It is advisable to plant and harvest early. Otherwise, it will ripen six or seven days after the Chinese wheat is harvested. What is not as good as planting early rice is this point. The area of our country affected by the flood is very wide. In the future, after the flood recedes, the need for wheat varieties will be huge. In the highlands where the flood has receded first, American wheat can be tried. Improving wheat varieties in this way is not a bad plan to avoid importing foreign wheat every year, which leads to an increasingly unsustainable economy. It is hoped that the ruling giants and patriotic heroes will study this article carefully. I sincerely implore them.

Correction: In the "Coffee Girl's Magic" article in the "Fuso Miscellany" column the other day, the three words "Napoleon" in the third line should be changed to "Columbus." We hereby declare this.

Records of What I've Seen and Heard in the Old Capital 148

— Zhu An

Fried Chestnuts

In various cities in the South today, around the Mid-Autumn Festival, fried chestnuts with sugar and sand are sold on the streets and alleys, labeled as "Liangxiang Chestnuts." Southerners are mostly vague about place names in the North. Only Liangxiang, with its fried chestnuts, has made an impression on everyone's minds. Liangxiang is the first county southwest of Beijing. The record of fried chestnuts in our country's history goes back thousands of years. According to the Qidan National Records, Xiao Han Jianu once said to the Liao Emperor, "I know how to fry chestnuts. If the small ones are cooked, the big ones will definitely be raw. If the big ones are cooked, the small ones will definitely be scorched." The Liao Dynasty used Yan as its southern capital. The Liao rulers must have been accustomed to the customs of Yanjing (Beijing), so Xiao Han Jianu used it as an analogy to make it easier for them to understand. Lao Xue An's Notes states, "Li He, who tossed chestnuts in the old capital, was famous in all directions. Others tried every means to imitate him, but they could never match him." His poem "Feeling About Eating Fried Chestnuts at Night in the Jiannan Collection" has a note saying, "Waiting for the morning court in a leaky house, officials often eat this." According to this, Bianjing (Kaifeng) also had this custom, and it was transmitted to Jiangbiao (Jiangnan) after the Southern Crossing. Then, such a small thing is related to the rise and fall of the world's fortune and the migration of culture over thousands of years. On a cold autumn night, next to a green lamp, buying a handful of this and eating it has a taste beyond taste, making one reflect on the past. In the Northern capital, fried chestnuts are followed by sweet potatoes. The roasted sweet potatoes are charred on the outside and cooked on the inside. Buying one and eating it while standing on the street can be a meal. The juice from the boiled sweet potatoes is thick and reddish in color and tastes especially rich. Whether rich or poor, everyone likes to eat them. Their fragrance is rich and mellow. Even wealthy people, passing by in a carriage, cannot help but smell it from afar and want to eat it.

Cat Calamity

It is said that the Persian cat is the best of all cat breeds. In our country, the Linqing lion cat is produced, which was valued by nobles in the past. The appearance of a lion cat is characterized by thick, shiny fur and the ability to sense human intentions. Every winter night, when warming oneself by the stove, having this creature curled up at one's feet is better than stroking jade-like skin. The North is bitterly cold, and short fur is not warm enough, so this breed is quite suitable. Its breed inheritance only appears every two or three generations. It is not necessarily true of every litter. Even in one litter, it only happens occasionally. My family's small calico cat produced one in its first litter. Its entire body was snow-white, except for half of its cheek and its tail, which were black. It was good at catching mice and also good at charming people. It was stroked all day long and never got annoyed. In the early spring of Bingyin year, it was sick for several days and did not eat. It was sent to the hospital, but the cause was unknown. It was thought that it could not be saved. Curling up by the stove, it suddenly got up and ate. Since then, it was able to recover. In the spring of Jiyi year, it suddenly disappeared. In recent years, the price of cat skin has been very high, worth several yuan per head. Greedy villains take advantage of the night to poison cats and lure them to their death. Families that raise cats hear about disappearances every day. After a long time, people gradually become aware. Although the police have also arrested and punished these people, no one can stop them where profit lies. There is no way to describe it other than calling it a cat calamity. Human nature is unkind and harms the innocent. Alas.

Novel Circulation Association

A Husband's Wife (18) 149

— Jiang Hongjiao

He took off the old gown he usually wore at home and put on a Western suit, preparing to visit some friends. However, the underarms of several Western suit jackets were torn and split. He sighed, opened the drawer, and looked for his wife's needle and thread, intending to mend them himself, but he couldn't find it. He had already taken out all the clothes he could wear this season and piled them on the bed, but they all had cracks. He resented his wife for being so irresponsible to her husband. The maid was from the countryside, and she couldn't sew this kind of clothes. He really had no choice, but he didn't want to go outside wearing torn clothes, so he could only abandon his plans to visit friends. He didn't bother to tidy up the clothes he had taken out, planning to let his wife see them when she got home in the evening, hoping she would feel bad and automatically mend them for him. He sat on the chair, sighing blankly, planning how to persuade his wife.

Mrs. Li suddenly walked in, holding a woman's photo in her hand. Her beautiful eyes were swollen and red, as she had been crying severely, with shiny tears still in her eyes.

"Mr. Chen! Look! This is a photo of a woman, the same woman who was in the car that night!" Mrs. Li handed the photo to Mr. Chen, panting and speaking with a sad tone.

"Really, it's a woman. Where did you get it?" Mr. Chen was also a little surprised.

"I got it from his pocket. Have you found out anything I asked you to investigate? You should help me."

"I don't dare to lie to you. I really haven't investigated it."

"Why didn't you go?"

"I don't have time during the day, and I'm too lazy to go out at night. Why don't you ask my wife to help you? She's been going to the movies with Mr. Li recently."

"Oh. Er is my close friend since childhood. In theory, she should help me, but I don't want to ask her. She's been too close to my husband recently, and she definitely won't investigate."

"Don't be discouraged. If you treat him so faithfully, he will surely realize it in the future. For now, try to be more tolerant and find less trouble for yourself, and it will be fine."

"You don't look good today. Are you feeling unwell? Oh! Why are there so many clothes piled on the bed?"

"It's nothing. I wanted to change clothes and go out, but I changed my mind at the last minute."

Mrs. Li began to tidy up the clothes one by one. Finally, she found the cracks. She went to get the needle and thread and mended each piece for him, hanging them back in the closet on hangers.
